BKA'-GDAMS-PA HISTORICAL NOTES



Bka!-gdans-pa Historical literature
Bka' gdams rin po che'i chos 'byung ram thar nyin mor byed pa'i 'od
stong zhes bya ba bzhugs s.ho
Manuscript (from Burmiok Athing's library)
ff. 94
Terminatur:
/bla ma'i mam thar nyin mor byed pa'i 'od stong zhes pa 'di ni/
rig gnas mtha' dag la mkhyen pa rgyas pa mkhan chen dge g.ye ba tshul
khrims seng ge'i gsung gis/ bka' gdams kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen byon
tshul mnams phyogs goig tu bsgrigs pa zhig gyis shes bskul kyang/ le
lo'i dbang gis re zhig 'gyangs pa la/ phyis don du gnyer ba'i bshes
gnyen 'ga' zhig gis 'phral phral du bskul bas mtshams sbyar te/ bde
bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab mtha' dag la mi 'jigs pa'i spobs pa brnyes
pa/ byams mgon 2 pa tshul khrims dar gyi zhabs rdul spyi bos bsten pa/
shākya'i dge slong bsod nams lha'i dbang pos khro mozhes pa shing
pho 'brug gi lo (1484)/ mngon bar byang chub pa'i zla ba yar ngo'i
tshes bcu la grub pa'i gnas mchog dpal ldan lo dgon pa'i dben gnas
dga' ldan rtser sbyar ba'o/
/'dis kyang rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che'i phyogs dus gnas
skabs thams cad (f. 93v) du dar zhing rgyas la yun ring du gnas pa'i
rgyur gyur cig/
dpal ldan bla ma'i thugs dgongs rdzogs pa dang/
mkha' myam 'gro la bỏe skyid 'byung ba dang/
/bdag gzhan ma lus tshogs rdzogs sgrib byang ste/
/myur du rdzogs pa'i byang chub thob par shog/...
Small mchan:
110 rgyus 'di rab byung brgyad pa shar nas lo so bdun 'das pa
shing 'brug lor (1484) mdzad par snang la deb sngon gyi me sprel
(1476) nas lo brgyad kyi dman pa ste bstan bcos kyi ngo bo rang bzo
chung la khungs che ba/ tshigs sbyor legs pa gcig tu snang bas
rtsigs su bya dgos ste bdag rig pa 'dzin pa tshe dbang nor bu'i dpe'o/
bkra shis dpal 'bar "dzam gling rgyan du shog/ sarba mangga lam/

Bsod-nams-lha-dbang: Bka' gdams chos 'byung
Mae'i srol 'dzin byon tshul la 3/ ra sgreng du byon tshul/ sku
mched 3 byon tshul/ de las 'phros pa byon tshul 10/
/dang po ni/ mal 'byor pa chen po ston pa yang lo dgu bsten/
ra sgreng gi gdan sa lo bcu gnyis mdzad pa'i ring dgon pa gong nas
phyir byon/ da lta dbu rtse ka ba bcu drug pa'i sa der gzims chung
mdzad/ de dus zhang 'phrang kha ber chung gi sras/ dgra bcom/ de'i
sras dar ma ye shes kyis/ ka 2 ma'i khyams smad/ khyams chung nag
tshang 3 mdzad de/ rab gnas rnal 'byor pa chen pos mdzad/ pa tra mang
du gtsugs/ gdul bya du ma smin par mdzad de/ dge 'dun sum brgya tsam
'dus/ drug bcu rtsa 2 pa 'brug lo rgyal zla'i tshes brgyad la ra
sgreng nas btegs/ dpe la lar rta lo pa yos la thegs pas bdun bcu
tham pa bzhugs zer ba yang snang ngo/
h /de nas dpal ldan DGON PA BA gdan sar bskos/ ston pa lo dgu
bsten/ rnal 'byor pa dang 'dra/ ra sgreng gi gdan sa lo bcu mdzad
(mchan: lo lnga yin nam)/ dgon pa gong ma rang du bzhugs nas/ sne'u
zur pa la sogs pa'i slob ma mang du smin par mdzad del drug bcu rtsa
bdun pa khyi lo'i mngon bar byang chub pa'i nya la ra sgreng nas
thegs/
dgon pa ba la slob ma mang du byon pa'i mchog bu chen bcu ni/
rlung shod rug pa'i zhang ka ma ba shes rab 'od/ kha rag sgom chung/
rog phyor phu ba smra ba'i seng ge/ mtha' 4 sgom pa/ 'phan yul rgyal
du gnyan sna mo ba dang/ 'bre ko te lung pa tshul khrims rgyal/ dar
yul du cho sgom gzhon nu snying po dang/ 'tshur sgom ye shes rgyal
mtshan 2/ 'phan yul snya ra dben tshar 'gar 'dul 'dzin/ spras thong
pa sar sne'u zur pa rnams so/
de mams kyi nang nas (1. 50v) chos brgyud 'dzin pa'i mchog
sne'u zur pa yin te cung zad 'og tu 'chad do/
/de rhams mal 'byor pa dang thun mong ba'i slob ma yin kyang/
dgon pa ba'i bu chen du drangs so/
KHA RAG SGOM CHUNG ni/ gtsang du sku 'khrungs/ lam po gnas su
mkhan po mar sgom la rab tu byung ste/ mtshan DBANG PHYUG BLO GROS
su btags/ dang por sbas sgom bsod nams rgyal mtshan (mchan: ye shes
yang zer) bya ba jo bo'i slob ma i la chos gsan/ de nas ra sgreng
du byon/ lo drug bzhugs nas/ mal 'byor pa dang/ dgon pa ba 2 la chos
mang du gsan/ gtsang bu'i thugs dgongs la da ni rang gis kyang tshig
kya thub ste 'ong snyam ste/ nyung mali sa bon phul gang khyer nas
sprags kyi sme'u ke tur byon/ dbyar lo thug gsol/ dgun nyung thug la
phye thun te btab nas gsol kyin lo bcu gcig tu sgrub pa rtse 1 mdzad/
de nas kha rag tu byon nas sgrub pa mdzad pas kha rag sgom chung du
grags/ kha 1 mtho chos dang/ ang yig bdun bcu rnams spragsu mdzad
zer te/ ram thar na kha rag shar du mdzad .gsungo/

Bsod-nams-lha-dbang: Bka' gdams chos 'byung
/3 pa de las 'phros pa byon (f. 57v) tshul la 2/ spo to ba nas
brgyud pa bka' gdams gzhung pa'i slob ma byon tshul/ spyan snga ba
nas brgyud pa bka' gdams gdams ngag pa'i slob ma byon tshul lo/
/dang po ni/ spo to ba la spyir slob ma mang du byon kyang
grags che ba mtha'i ka chen brgyad/ dbus kyi nyi zla zung 1 ces pa
ltar na/ gtsang du ram snang 2/ gnyal du glang gnyos 2) dol du 'be
rog 2/ khams su bya phag 2/ dbus su glang shar 2 rnams yin la/
bka' babs brgyad du byed na/ bya phag 2 mi 'dren par/ byams
snying rje byang chub kyi sems bdag gzhan brje nus pa'i bka' glang
ri thang pa rdo rje seng ge la babs/ bka' 'gyur ro cog la gzhung béad
byed pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la mnga' brnyes pa 'dra ba yod
pa'i bka' shar ba pa yon tan grags la babs/ gsung rab thams cad skyes
bu 3 gyi gdams ngag tu dril nas sman pa mkhas pas nad brtags te nad
thog tu sman gtong ba 'dra ba yod pa'i bka'/ snang tre'u lhas pa ye
shes rgyal mtshan la babs/stong nyid kyi lta bas dngos po dang mtshan
mar 'dzin pa thams cad 'jig nus pa yod pa'i bka' ram sding ma ba
'byung gnas rdo rje la babs/
rtsod pa pandi ta'i rgol ba yang bzlog nus pa yod pa'i bka'/ dol
pa shes rab rgya mtsho la babs/ bla ma la sangs rgyas dngos kyi mos
gus rgyun chad med pa yod pa'i bka'/ gnyal pa chos 'bar la babs/
dang tshugs mchog zung 1 la 'gran nus pa yod pa'i bka'/ grab pa gzhon
nu 'od (yon tan 'od yang zer) la babs/ rgyun du dkon mchog gi drung
du mchod pa bkra lam me ba 'bul ba yod pa'i bka' / dge bshes bras dkar
ba la babs so/
/de yang GLANG RI THANG PA ni/ 'khrungs sa 'phan yul gnya' gong
gser ma bshongs (f. 58r) yab jo bo dar ma mdo bzang gi sras su shing
pho rta (1054) la 'khrungs/ rus zhugs tshang/ kho rang gi zhang po
bshes gnyen grog mo mkhar pa la rab tu byung/ mtshan RDO RJE SENG GEr
btags/ rgyal ba 'od dpag tu med pa'i sprul par byed la sngon lo tsā
ba ka ba dpal brtsegs su sprul nas bstan pa ches cher gsal bar mdzad
cing/ 'dir gdul bya blo dman pa mnams kyi ngor/ dang po shin tu bkren
pa'i tshul mdzad de/ lo na spyan snga la chos gsan dus yos sbar ba
res gdan gnon md zad kyi bzhugs/
de nas bsod snyoms mdzad pa'i rñed pa gang byung/ spyir dge 'dun
dang khyad par spo to ba doon slob la drangs pas sku bsod skyes pa
ltar mdzad de/ gra pa nyid stong tsam 'tshogs pa'i rgyags khong rang
gis gnang/ gnas nges med du bshad sgrub zung 'brel du mdzad/ gtso bor
spo to ba yun ring du bsten/ phu chung ba dang/ kham pa lung ca chen
po sogs la yang chos gsan/ spo to ba gshegs nas thang grong Itag tu
gtor ma mdzad dus/ gtor sder bya rog gis khyer te glang thang gi shar



Bsod-nams-lha-d bang: Bka' gdams chos 'byung
ri de'u de'i khar gzhag pas/ dpon shāk bya bas zhabs tog byas te der
lo 3 sgrub pa mdzad/ zhol du sgrub chu yang byung/ nyin mtshan dbyer
med du byang chub kyi sems kyi ting nge 'dzin bsgoms pa'i mdangs la/
klu mo spun 3 gyis glang thang gi gnas phul/ dge 'dun gyi sde 'dzugs
par zhus/ phyis ri de'i steng nas yar 'phur te thugs phreng skyur sar
khron pa brus/ dbu zhwa skyur sar bla brang byas te dgon pa btab/ slob
ma mang du 'dus/ bka' gdams gzhung drug lam sgron sogs la 'chad nyan
mdzad cing/ bdag gzhan brje ba'i byang chub (f. 58v) kyi sems kho na
la gtso bor mdzad de/ kho bos rlung tha mal du gtong ma myong gsung/
zhal bzhugs rin glang thang gi lcags ri'i nang du srog chags mnams 1
la 1 mi 'tshe bar grags/ dgung lo bdun bcu pa chu mo yos (1123) kyi
sa ga zla ba la dpe'i chos lung du sku gshegs/
RGYA LCAGS RI GONG KHA BA BYANG CHUB DPAL ni/ khamsu glang ri
thang pa'i snyan pa thos pas/ dbus su chos la 'byon pa'i 'dun pa yod
pa/ srin mo zhig gi gnod pas/ pho bo drug 'das/ khong rang yang sngags
kyis bcings te khyi'i lus su bsgyur yang/ glang ri thang pa dang mjal
bar 'gron po'i phyi la yongs/ srin mos mnan du sleb pa na/ glang ri
thang pas mkhyen pas der byon bgegs bskrad/ gtor mas byin gyis brlabs
pas mi'i lus su gyur/ stong nyid snying rje thugs su chud de slob
ma'i mchog tu gyur/ jo bo'i slob ma bshes gnyen bal bo bas btab pa'i
lcags ri gong khar bzhugs pas rgya lcags ri bar grags so/
/gzhan yang slob ma che ba/ dge bshes lcags zhing pa/ khyung po
mal 'byor/ ra lo tsā ba/ gnyan chen po/ zhang zhung mdo sde la sogs
byon la/ gdan sa shara bas glang thang dang shar ba sbrel nas/ dge
'dun sum stong tsam 'dus/ de nas gdan sa zhang zhung pas mdzad/ mchod
rten chen mo drang srong gis bskul te bzhengs tshul dang/ bar du rin
chen sgang pas bdag byas pa sogs rgyas par ma spros so/
/ZHANG SHAR BA PA CHEN PO ni/ pa tshab rom pa'i rgyud du lcags
khyi (1070) la) yum phyugs bskyong ba'i dus/ rdo leb steng du 'khrungs
te/ de la zhabs rjes kyang byon/ dgung lo bco brgyad pa la klung
shod phyor bar bros te rab tu byung/ mtshan yon tan grags su btags/
de nas spyan snga ba phyor phur sku mtshams (f. 59r) md zad pa'i sar
mjal/ zla ba 4 mtshams khrod du bzhugs te chos gsan/ da nga'i grogs
po'i rtsar brgyugsung bas/ stag lung du spo to ba'i spyan sngar byon/,
gra pa lo dug/ nang mi lo dgu ste bowa brgyad bsten/ zhar la phu chung
pa dang/ spyan snga ba la yang 'dod chos rdzogs par gsan/ spo to ba
gshegs nas yon tan gyi rjes su 'brang ba'i 'khor mams dang lhan cig
klung shod du byon te tshogs pa bsdus/ de nas gnas nges med du 'chad
nyan mdzad pas/ gra pa nyis stong brgyad brgya tsam 'dus/ de rnams phal
cher chos don gnyer sha stag go/

Bsod-nams-lha-dbang: Bka' gdams chos 'byung
de yang bshes gnyen ston pa/ mor pa/ dgon pa ba/ sku mched
gsum/ sne'u zur pa) shar ba pa mams la BKA' GDAMS ZHAL BRGYAD du
grags so/
/snang dre'u lhas pa'i mam thar ma mthong zhing/ ram sding ma
ba 'byung gnas rdo rje'i mam thar che chung 3 'dug pa'i skye ba bcu
drug pa'i mam thar du/ bdag nyid ting nge 'dzin la mnyam par bzhag
tsa na/ bskal pa stong gi skye ba dran te/ yab yum bla ma dang/ chos
gang la zhus pa/ rus dang rigs dang/ gnas dang phyogs thams cad kyang
dran/ dus rgyun du sa le ba ni skye ba bcu drug dran no zhes gsung
la/ gtsang smad du ram sding ma'i chos sde btab/ gzhi bdag gis mdzo
mo dkar mo 1 phul ba sa la thim pas/ chu mig khyad par can zhig byung
ste/ rgya gar gyi mda' chu khron pa skyes dang khyad med) sus 'thungs
kyang rgyal gsung/ gra pa stong tsam byung/
slob ma 1 la khyod lho brag tu song/ 'di kho na 'dra ba'i sa
cha yod/ der dgon pa thob/ bla ma dang dgon pa'i ming yang 1 pa thogs
gsung ste/ lho brag sding ma de las brgyud do/
DOL PA SHES RAB RGYA MTSHO ni/ jo bo dol du phebs dus/ yul 'di
nas brad med (read: byang chub sems dpa') rtags mtshan ca zhig (f. 59v)
'byung/ zhes lung bstan tel sa pho 'brug (1028) la 'khrungs/ yang
zhogs gad kyi dgon pa btab/ spo to ba'i gsung la zin bris su mdzad
pa phyis phyogs 1 tu bsgrigs pa la/ be'u bum sngon por grags pa mdzad/
chos brgyud 'dzin pa'i mchog don stengs pa chos skyabs bzang po dang/
lha 'bri sgang pa chen po sogs byon/
don stengs pas glo'i phur don stengs btab nas gra thang dang
sbrags nas bzung/ lha 'bri sgang pas be'u bum sngon po la 'grel pa
legs pa 1 mdzad de phrin las che zhing/ 'on gyi phur 'bri sgang gi
dgon pa btab/ tshogs pa'ang mang du 'dus/ bar skabs su 'bri sgang gi
dgon bdag bya yul bas mdzad nas mkhan po'i bko gzhag kyang mang du
mdzad snang ngo/
/'BE SE DKAR BAs gzhung gi mdar ra brags kyi gtsug lag khang
btab/ mkhan brgyud shin du 'phel bar byung ngo/
/GRAB PA GZHON NU 'OD (YON TAN 'OD yang zer) ni/ 'phan yul grab
tu 'khrungs/ bzhugs gnas grab phu'i phrong sdings te/ khong rang
gzhon nu nas thos pa che bas/ dang por spo to ba la chos kyi tshod
bltar byon kyang/ phyis mi phyed pa'i dad pa skyes te/ ikog chos lo
bcu drug gsan/ spo to ba'i gsung sgros bsgrigs pa'i dpe chos rtsa
grel mdzad do/
/DGE BSHES BRAG DKAR BA spre'u lo la/ 'khor 4 brgya tsam 'dus/
dpe chos gsan pa'i ched du grab pa'i slob ma mdzad/ dgung lo brgyad
bcu pa yos lo'i dgun zla tha chung gi nyer 2 la thegs/ de'i slob ma

sgom/ de'i slob ma skyer sgang pa la sogs byon no/

Bsod-nams-lha-dbang: Bka' gdams chos 'byung
(1175) zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes Inga la mtha' phur thegs/ gdung
bzhu bas thugs ljags sogs byon/ gser gyi me tog gi char bab par grags
te/ rgyas par blo sbyong gi byung tshul dang mam thar che chung du
blta'o/
/de'i khyad par gyi sras SE SPYIL PHU BA ni/ 'khrungs yul ido
stod zer gnyal stod dar ma sgang/ gdung rus se/ dgung snying Icags
mo glang (1121)/ rab byung dang bsnyen rdzogs 2 ka'i mkhan po phya

61r) ba dang mjal/ yun ring du bsten cing yon tan bum pa gang byo'i
tshul du mdzad/ sngar bya mchad kyis lung bstan pa bzhin mchad kha
gsar ma btab/ mchad kha ba chen po'i nang rten du sku ider rin po che
dang/ phyi rten gyi mchod rten la sogs pa bzhengs nas klungs shod du
byon/ spyil phu'i dgon pa btab ste/ mam g•yeng spangs nas stod du
mkhar gong la kha/ smad du nyung zhing sgang du mtshams mtho brgyab
nas lo bdun du mtshams mi 'da' mdzad/
bela de nas brag dkar gnas brtan sogs kyis spyan drangs nas/ mchad
khar dgun chos la byon pas/ ding sang gi bar dbyar gyi tshul zhugs
spyil phur mdzad/ dgun chos mchad khar gsung ba'i srol byung la/ gdul
bya du ma smin par mdzad nas/ drug bcu rtsa dgu pa sa mo bya'i lo

slob ma'i mchog lha chen po rgya spang pa thang pa/ nyan lha sdings
pa sogs mang du byon pa las/
LHA CHEN PO ni/ yab jo bo mor/ yum snam nam gza'i sras su
stag lo ( ) la pho trang khang dmar du 'khrungs/ dgung lo bwa
Inga la rgya dur gyi mkhan po klubs dkar dang/ gtsang pa khyung po la
mkhan slob zhus/ bya sar rab tu byung ste mtshan BYANG CHUB RIN CHEN
du btags/ de nas bya mchad kha ba'i sku 'dra gzigs pas dad pa'i rkyen
byas te/ dge bshes se dang mjal/ chos mang du zhus/ nyi shu rtsa 4 la
rgya sar sgang nas mkhan po glan spyan drangs te bsnyen par rdzogs/
gzhan yang kha che pan chen la sogs pa bla ma mang du bsten/ se spyil
bu ba gshegs nas/ mchad kha spyil phu'i gdan sa mdzad/ bka' 'gyur gyi
lung bzhugs pas lha lung gi dbang phyug gi ru grags/ sangs rgyas sman

Bsod-nams-lha-dbang: Bka' gdams chos 'byung
dpon nā ga bo dhi dang mjal ba bden nam zhus pas/ btsun chung 'di 'drir
bcug pa'i chos mi 'dra ba gsung/ phyis gshegs kar ngas slob dpon nā ga
bo dhi dang dngos su mjal/ chos mang du zhus/ rtsa ba'i bla mar byed
pa yin khyed rang yang gsol ba thob dang rjesu 'dzin par 'dug gsung/
mdor na spyan snga ba'i yon tan bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mnga' zhing/
spyan snga ba smyug rum du gshegs nas sku gdung bzhu ba'i dus thugs
nam mkha' laa 'od dang (f. 66v) bcas te/ sprul sku chen po'i dpang par
babs pa phyis bya yul gyi gdung khang du bzhugso/
/smyug rum du sku mtshams lo dgu mdzad/ de nas tshogs bsdus te/
thog mar brul gyi ra ba dkar por dgon pa btab/ dge 'dun Inga brgya
tsam 'dus/ de'i tshe rje btsun ma sgrol ma la sogs yi dam mang po'i
zhal gzigs/ nā ga bo dhi la dngos su chos gsan/ de nas gdul bya bsam
gyis mi khyab pa dang/ dgon pa 'bul ba yang mang du byung ba la/ bla.
ma dang sgrol mas lung bstan pa'i gnas bya yul du dgon pa 'debs dgongs
kyang/ yon bdag mnams the tshom bsal ba'i phyir/ bshes gnyen mtha'
bzhi spyan drangs nas dgon pa thams cad nas rdo rje blangs pa la sa
dpyad mdzad nas/ se gsal ba'i g.yung drung gis phul ba/ bya yul nas
blangs pa'i rdo rje la sa'i dpyad bzang bar lung bstan pas/ gzhan mams
kyang ma dga' ba med par mdzad/ lo dgon pa btab nas/ lo nyi shu rtsa
gnyis pa shing pho rta'i lo ( ) gtsug lag khang gi mang bting nas/
lo bcu 3 pa rta lo'i nang tshun la dgon pa gtor tshugs yan rdzogs par
grub/ rmang bting nas na ning chu mo yos (1483) yan la 'das lo sum
brgya dang bdun beu song ngo/
De /de'i tshe spyan snga ba rnal lam du byon nas snam sbyar gser
mdog can bkon pa rmis pas/ bla mas gnang ba byung gsung nas/ mkhan po
mngog (or: rdog) chos dbang/ las slob mang ra sgom pa/ gsang ston rgya
shes rab 'bar gyis mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ bya yul du dge 'dun
nyis stong lnga brgya tsam 'dus/
de dus bya yul/ klung shod/ mal gro 3 du dus 1 la gral dbu mdzad
pa dang/ mdo smad du ngang tshang ba'i gtsug lag khang gi rab gnas
dang/ dags por sha ba gling pa'i mchod rten gyi (f. 67r) rab gnas zhus
pas dus tshod tshes grangs 'di la mchod pa rgya chen po bshoms/ gsol
ba thob/ ngas gzims chung 'di'i steng nas rab gnas byed pa yin gsung
ste/ kun gyis mthong bar gtsug lag khang dang/ mchod rten stengs su
phyag nas babs pas/ de nas sprul skur grags/ mi ma yin mang po la
chos gsungs pa dang/ skyed rdzogs kyi rtogs pa mnga' ba/ mngon shes

Bsod-nams-lha-dbang: Bka' gdams chos 'byung

Bsod-nams-lna-dbang: Bka' gdams chos 'byung
pa'i rim pa/ gser gling pas jo bo la gnang ba'i rtog pa 'bur 'joms
rtsa 'grel/ blo sbyong lhan thabs 4 pa/ de'i sgo nas sdig pa bshags
pa dang/ 'khon sbyang ba'i cho ga/ ku sā li'i tshogs sog/ blo sbyong
kun tu bzang po/ blo sbyong stan thog 1 ma/ blo sbyong thun brgyad
ma/ glang ri thang pa'i tshig rkang brgyad ma/ de'i 'grel pa bya ston
gyis mdzad pa/ blo sbyong rten 'brel snying po dang/ bka' gdams thor
bu ba sogs dang/ gzhan yang rgyal po sa'i sam ghas zhus pa'i bod kyi
mnam gzhag sogs mang du snang ngo/
/3 pa 'phrin yig gi skor la/ jo bos mdzad pa glong du bshad la/
lo tsā ba rin chen bzang pos sku mtshams nas grogs po mnams la springs
pa/ dge bshes ston pas jo bo spyan 'dren pa'i dus/ mnga' ris nas bod
ston mnams la springs pa tshigs su bcad pa bcu dgu pa/ zhang 'phreng
kha ber chung la springs pa snga (f. 89r) phyi 2/ sgom chen byang
chub la springs pa/ bshes gnyen blo gros 'byung gnas la springs pa/
a mes sman rgan sogs la gdams pa'o/

pa/ yung ba'i chang 'thung mams la springs pa/ bya yul gyi mchod

so/

pa gdams ngag tshig drug ma dang/ dge bshes dbang seng la springs pa/

blo ldan la springs pa/ mchod gnas dbang nge la springs pa/ sha bo
sgang pa la springs pa/ sgom chen seng ge sgra la springs pa sogs shar

rnams kyi skye ba dran pa tsam la yon tan du mi mdzad/ sbas pa'i gter
bsrung sla ba bzhin du/ yon tan thams cad nang du sbed pa yin/ bla

pas/ gtsug tor du/ bcad do/ phur bus gdab po bya ba de bgegs la nus
pa med par byed pa yin/

ma 4n du 'gro bas/ tshig zin par bya/ don go bar bya/ rtogs pa rgyud
la skyes par bya) yi ger mi bri bar bya gsung nas/ phyag dar la nan

ba mnams kyis kyang rnam thar rgyas pa ma bkod cing/ gdul bya thun
mong ba dang bstun pa'i rnam thar mdor bsdus tsam dang/ 'das dus ngos
'dzin gyi yi ge che chung ma gtogs/ mam thar phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs
pa (f. 92v) ma mthong bas/ thun mong ba gang mthong mnams 'dir phyogs
gcig tu mdor bsdus te dad pa'i blos bkod pa'o/

/thugs rje'i byin brlabs gting mtha' mi mngon phrin las rnam
bzhi'i rba brlabs rgyun chad med par g.yo bas brjid/
/mam dag 1ta ba'i rin chen mchog gi cod pan dang ldan snying
rje'i klu dbang spyan zur rol pas mdzes/
/brgyad khri bzhi stong chos kyi bcud ldan mam thar mtsho chen
'di ni 'gro ba'i dpal du rgyas gyur cig/

/thub bstan padmo'i bzhin ras gsal mdzad pa/

legs bshad 'di ni sngon med gangga'i rgyun/
kha cig rgyal dang mkhas mams gang bzhed pa'i/

/zhugs kyang de don bsgrub par mi nus shing/

/bstan dang 'gro la phan par dgongs mams kyis/

/sngon byung skyes chen dam pa de dag gi/

/zab mo ita bas 'khrul pa'i mtshan ma zhi/

/nyams len sgom pas sems nyid rang sar grol/
/rgya chen spyod pas phyin drug lam du 'khyer/

/ngo mtshar sbrang rtsi'i longs spyod 'di sbyar bas/
/don gnyer bung ba'i dga' ston rgyas gyur cig/

ni/ rig gnas mtha' dag la mkhyen pa rgyas pa mkhan chen dge g.ye ba
tshul khrims seng ge'i gsung gis/ bka' gdams kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen
byon tshul mams phyogs goig tu bsgrigs pa zhig gyis shes bskul kyang/
le lo'i dbang gis re zhig 'gyangs pa la/ phyis don du gnyer ba'i
bshes gnyen 'ga' zhig gis 'phral 'phral du bskul bas mtshams sbyar
te/ bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab mtha' dag la mi 'jigs pa'i spobs
pa brnyes pa/ byams mgon 2 pa tshul khrims dar gyi zhabs rdul spyi
bos bsten pa/ shākya'i dge slong bsod nams lha'i dbang pos khro mo

rgyur gyur cig/

(11th cent)
snang/ rim pa ma byas kyang byang chub kyi sems (f. 75v) brtan
po yod na de kun nyan du rung gsung/ phyi de nyin khri khar
byon nas/ ngas bla ma la zhus pas 'di skad gsung gsungs nas

sha'i gnang ba 'di ches so bya ba'i tshig smras kyang mdzad
skad/ jo bo lo bcu bsten cing/ lam rim shlo ka drug dang/ de'i
gsal byed mdzad/ spyir jo bo'i chos mang du mkhyen yang dbu
ma'i Ita ba la rtsal thon/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma'i zhal gzigs/
lan gcig jo bo'i phyag phyir byon pas/ gsang phu la phyag
mdzub btsugs te/ lung pa ya gi'i nang a na dung g.yas su
'khyil ba 'dra ba yod/ legs she khyod kyis der gtsug lag khang
thob la bshad nyan gyis dang bstan pa la phan thogs rgya chen
'byung zhes lung bstan pa bzhin gsang phu ne'u thog tu gtsug
lag khang btab/ bshad nyan mdzad pas tshogs pa lnga brgya tsam
'dus so/
/gsang phu ba'i zhal nas/ chos bzhi dang ldan na gcig pur
gnas kyang mi nyams shing dkar po'i chos 'phel bar gsungs te/
bzhi gang zhe na/ man ngag la rang dbang thob pa dang/ gnod pa
phra mo sel nus pa dang/ dad pas khams brtas pa dang/ tshul
khrims la ngo lkog mtshugs pa'o/ /zhes gsungs te/ 'di la gro
lung pas gdams pa'i don por mdzad do/
/de'i dbon po RNGOG LO CHEN PO ni/ chos bskyabs kyi sras
su sa mo phag (1059) la sku 'khrungs/ gzhon nu'i dus nas khu

Akam ka na'i gzungs kyi bar do la chu sbyin byed par gang nas
kyang ma bshad dol.
/yang tshogs bdag gi gzung bya ba cig dang/ tshogs bdag gis
rgyud



ces bya ba le'u bcu gnyis pa cig yod de/ de cha tshogs bdag phyag
gnyis pa dang phyag bzhi pa la sogs pa'i rigs kha yar gyi bsgrub
thabs dang/ dbang bskur ba dang/ drag po'i las sbyor la sogs pa
ston te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su gtogs par snga ma mnams
bzhed del
dpal nag po chen po'i rgyud the tsom za ba cig gda'/ ces bya
ba le'u brgyad pa cig yod de/ dpal ldan phyag drug pa'i sgos kyi
rgyud yin la/ rgyal po mig mi bzang gi zhus shing/ rta mgrin gyi
gsung pa'o/
/'di kha cig de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su gtogs par bzhed la/
kha cig rta mgrin gyi gsungs pa phyag drug pa nyid kyang spyan
rag gzigs yin pa'i phyir/ padma'i rigs su gtogs zhes bshad do/
/padma'i rigs kyi rgyud la/ rigs kyi gtso bo/ bdag po/ yum/
khro bo khro mo/ bka' nyan pho mo rgyud sde Inga'o/
/rigs kyi gtso bo'i rgyud ni/ bcom idan 'das kyi mnyan yod
du 'jam dpal la gsungs pa ste/ phyogs kyi tshe dpag med kyi
mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa yon tan bsngags pa dang bcas pa ste/
de la om gsum ma cig dang/ om gnyis pa su ni zhes pa'i sngags
tshan med ba cig dang gnyis yod de/ de gnyis las cig las bde ba
can gyi tshe dpag med zer/ gcig la 'og min gyis tshe dpag med zer
ba mi 'thad do/
Ignyis ka steng phyogs kyi tshe dpag med



Rgya gar chos 'byung: Ka
kyi gzungs su gsungs pa'i phyir te/ om gnyis ma la sngags bar
du 'chad pas/ mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad ma tshang ba yin gyis/
rgyud so so ba gnyis min no/
/tshe dpag med kyi 'chi med mnga sgra'i gzungs zhes bya ba/
bcom idan 'das kyi dge slong rnams la/ bde ba can gyi tshe dpag
med kyi mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad yon tan bsngags pa dang bcas
pa gsungs tel de la sogs pa rams so/
/rigs kyi bdag po'i rgyud ni/ spyan ras gzigs kyi rtsa
rgyud chen po/ thugs rje chen po padma dra ba'i rgyud ces bya
ba'o/ /bcom ldan 'das ri bo po ta lar gsungs pa'i le'u bcu gnyis
pa de las bcu gcig zhal lha stong nyi brgya bzhi bcu rtsa bdun
gyi dkyil 'khor la sogs pa'o/
/rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor nyi shu rtsa bdun de las 'phros pa'i
dkyil 'khor du ma ston pa cig/
laon yod zhags pa'i cho ga zhib mo'i rgyud ces bya ba/ bcom
idan 'das ri bo ta la'i rtser gsungs pas/ bsgur 'phros ma lus
par bam po nyi shu rtsa bzhi pa cig yod de/ gzung dang cho ga
zhib mo dang/ las tshogs du ma dang bcas pa gsung par ston to/
/yang don yod zhags pa'i gzung chung ba cig yod pa ni/
cho ga zhib mo'i rgyud kyi stod kyi gzungs kyi sgor zur du bkol
ba yin gyis rgyud zur pa ma yin no/
de'i sham du khrus chog yod med gnyis yod la yang rgyud
so so ma yin cing/ sngon gyi bla ma dag gis khrus chog



zin ris mdzad pa rgyud zer bkol/
de'i zlar shor ba yin gyis rgya gar nas 'gyur ba yang ma
yin no/
/phyag stong spyan stong gi cho ga zhib mo'i rgyud ces bya
ba rgyud chen po/ bcom ldan 'das kyi po ta lar gsungs pa cig
'gyur ba 'phro lùs zhig yod do/
de las dkyil 'khor cig bstan to/
/spyan ras gzigs seng ge sgra'i gzungs che chung gnyis yod
del chung ba rdo rje gdan du gsungs/ che ba rgyal sa dbang phyug
'od ces bya ba mdze nad kyi zin pa gso ba'i don du 'phags pa
'jam dpal gyis zhus te/ cha bcom idan 'das kyi ri bo ta lar
gsungs te de la sogs pa'i spyan ras gzigs kyi skor mang du
yod pa mams so/
to /rigs kyi yum gyi rgyud ni/ gtso che ba de bzhin gshegs pa
thams cad yum sgrol ma las sna tshogs 'byung rgyud ces bya ba
le'u sum bcu rtsa Inga pa cig yod del de'i le'u gsum pa las
sgrol ma'i bstod pa phyag 'tshal nyi shu rtsa gcig rgya skad
sor bzhag tu yod de/ kha cig de dang phyag 'tshal nyi shu rtsa
gcig zur du bsgyur ba gsum don ma gcig/ zur du bsgyur ba'i bla
med kyi rgyud las yin tel slob dpon nyi ma sbas pas bla med du
bkral baso/ /zhes zer yang/ 'grel byed kyi de ltar bkral bas de
don mi cig mi dgos te/ 'jam dpal mtshan brjod slob dpon sgeg
pa'i rdo rje dang/ ngag dbang grags pas yo gar bkral dus 'khor
gyi 'grel chen du bkral/
'phags pa lhas kyang/

Rgya gar chos 'byung: Karo
113
grags so/

byas/ sa hyer chos kyi rdo rje mchog tu mtshan gsol ba/ gtsug tor

dag pa'i gi tshul/ /'jig rten mal 'byor cho gas slob dpon bzhin
rims kyi/ /'di ni yun ring gnas phyir bdag gis mam par bsam/ /zhes
so/
/slob dpon des thun mong gis dngos grub thob par grags shing/
des yul kan tra ko sa lar dpal ldan bde byed kyi byas pa'i gtsug
lag khang na rgyal po dpa' bo zhes bya bas sbyin bdag mdzad nas
gnas pa'i tshe/ grong gnas brtan abang po'i go chas bskul zhing/
slob ma shes rab lha'i don du de nyid bsdus pa'i rgya cher bshad
pa sho lo ka stong phrag bcu gnyis pa de mdzad de mtshan yang
ko sa la'i rgyan du grags so/
/de nyid las/
yon tan mang dang ldan pa mchog gi gnas gyur gando sngon
'gro ka sa la/ /dge zhing tshul mang legs pa rgya mtsho dang
ldan gtsug lag khang mchog de/ /dpal ldan bde byed kyi



Rgya gar chos 'byung: Ka
114
byas shin tu yid 'ong mkhas pa mnams kyi gnas gyur cing/ /rgyal
po dpa' bo'i chos kyi bdag nyid dpal gyi kha ba bzhin bsil der
gnas tshe/ /dang por grogs mchog gnas brten dbang po'i cho ga'i
tshig gi gsol ba btab pa dang/ /shes rab lha'i mkhas bcas brtson
pa'i stobs sogs gtso bo byas la brten pa dang/ /bde gshegs pa
bstan la khro bo 'di dag nyon mongs dbang po mthong ba dang/
/skyon med gsang sngags don yang gzhan dbang song bas gzhan du
kun tu sbyor bar 'gyur/ /de phyogs nges don shin tu mam 'byed
tshig don gsal zhing kun gyi thun mong ba'i/ /rgya cher bshad
'di 'gro ba'i don du kun 'grub phyir shākya mi tras sa steng
brtsams/ /zhes so/
/yang dang pa'i slob dpon 'jam dpal gyi grub thob de dang
mi mtshungs pa'i slob dpon gsang bas/ dang por thos pa tsam ma
mdzad par bal yul du ud pa la phung po cig dang/ ba dmar ser gyi
mar skyog gang dang/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sku ras ris gcig
dang gsum mdun du bzhag ste bsgrub pa la/ dus nam zhig na me tog
kyang kha bye/ mar yang khol/ ras bris kyang bzhed pa mthong ba
la/ slob dpon gyi dngos grub len ma mkhyen te/ mar btung ngam/
me tog dbul lam/ go rim gang yin snyam du rtog par gyur pa las/
rtog pa de nyid gegs su gyur te/ gnod sbyin mo yaksha 'gram zhes
bya bas



slob dpon gyi 'gram pa la thal cag gsol bas/ slob dpon brgyal bar
gyur to/
/de nas brgyal ba sogs tsam na/ rnying pa dang/ bo ba dang/
sku la rdol gyis go bar gzigs so/
no /de nas mar lhag ma 'thung/ me tog phul/ sku'i rdul phyis
nas bzhugs so/
de ltar gyur kyang dngos grub phra mo thob ste/ shes rab
shin tu rno bar gyur nas/ e ma bdag ltar thos pa chung ba yang/
bdud kyi las su rig par bya'o/ /gsung nas grong khyer mnyan yod
kyi slob dpon chen po padma rdo rje'i myu gu zhabs la gsan pas
mkhyen rab kyi phul du gyur te grong khyer ser skya'i nags khrod
du bzhugs nas 'grel pa yang btags/ mang du gsungs pa la/ 'dul
bas g.yeng bar rig nas/ e ma bdag Itar thos pa che ba yang bdud
kyi las su rig par bya'o/ gsung nas su rang du byon gangs ti se'i
drung du bsgrub pa mdzad pas phyag rgya chen po'i dngos grub
brnyes so/
/de ltar na dngos grub rgyud la mkhas pa'i mi gsum/ don la
mkhas pa sangs rgyas gsang ba/ tshig la mkhas pa shākya bshes gnyen/
tshig don gnyis ka la mkhas pa kun dga' snying po zhes sam/ rig
pa la mkhas pa shākya bshes gnyen/ man ngag la mkhas pa sangs rgyas |
gsang ba/ gnyis ka'i sgo nas lag len la mkhas pa kun dga' snying po/
mkhas pa mi gsum grags so/
Akun dga' snying po'i mched grogs/ slob dpon 'jam dpal grags
pa ste/ de'i sku che ba'i yon tan inga dang ldan pa ste/ 'jig
rten pa'i rigs kyi mchog
